â”‚  Data Analysis Plan for Market Sizing and Competitive Analysis on Residential Whole Home Generator Servicing:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  1. **Data Sources**:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚     - **Census Bureau**: Demographic information relevant to household incomes and potential market size.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚     - **Bureau of Labor Statistics (BLS)**: Data on employment rates in the energy and utilities sectors.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚     - **Energy Information Administration (EIA)**: Reports on energy consumption and trends.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚     - **Industry Reports**: Research from firms like IBISWorld, Statista, or similar sources.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚     - **SEC Filings**: Financial performance data from publicly traded companies involved in the generator market.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  2. **Data Cleaning and Structuring Approach**:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚     - Remove duplicates from datasets.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚     - Standardize formats for dates and currency.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚     - Appropriately handle missing values (imputation or removal).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚     - Encode categorical variables correctly.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  3. **Analysis Methodology**:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚     - Use descriptive statistics to summarize the dataset.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚     - Perform trend analysis on historical data to identify growth patterns.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚     - Use cluster analysis to identify segments within the market.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚     - Create visualizations (e.g., line graphs, bar charts) for clear representation of findings.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  4. **Documentation of Data Sources and Limitations**:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚     - Document each data source detailing its relevance to the project.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚     - Identify potential biases or limitations within each dataset.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  Conceptual Analysis Plan:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  ```python                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  import pandas as pd                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚  import matplotlib.pyplot as plt                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  # Load hypothetical data                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  census_data = pd.read_csv('census_data.csv')  # Demographic data                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚  bls_data = pd.read_csv('bls_data.csv')  # Employment statistics                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚  eia_data = pd.read_csv('eia_data.csv')  # Energy consumption data                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  # Data cleaning                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚  def clean_data(df):                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚      df.drop_duplicates(inplace=True)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚      df.fillna(method='ffill', inplace=True)  # Simple forward-fill for missing values                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚      return df                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  census_data = clean_data(census_data)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  bls_data = clean_data(bls_data)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚  eia_data = clean_data(eia_data)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  # Analysis -- Basic summary statistics                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚  summary_stats = census_data.describe()                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚  print(summary_stats)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  # Visualization                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚  plt.figure(figsize=(10,5))                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚  plt.plot(census_data['Year'], census_data['Household_Income'], label='Household Income')                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  plt.title('Household Income Over Years')                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  plt.xlabel('Year')                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  plt.ylabel('Income')                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  plt.legend()                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  plt.show()                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚  ```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   â”‚
